I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[exclude-newer]: Workspace level takes precedence over channel
### Checks

- [x] I have checked that this issue has not already been reported.

- [x] I have confirmed this bug exists on the [latest version](https://github.com/prefix-dev/pixi/releases/latest) of pixi, using `pixi --version`.


### Reproducible example

On current unreleased main:
```toml
[workspace]
channels = [
    { channel = "conda-forge", exclude-newer = "3y"},
    { channel = "bioconda", exclude-newer = "1y"},
    { channel = "https://prefix.dev/github-releases", exclude-newer = "2d"}] # doesn't work
platforms = ["osx-arm64", "linux-64", "linux-aarch64", "osx-64", "win-64"]
# Takes precedence over the channel-level setting
exclude-newer = "1y"

[dependencies]
python = "*"
chainsaw = "*" # from github-releases
```

Results in:
```
❯ pixi lock
Error:   × failed to solve requirements of environment 'default' for platform 'osx-arm64'
  ├─▶   × failed to solve the environment
  │   
  ╰─▶ Cannot solve the request because of: The following packages are incompatible
      └─ chainsaw * cannot be installed because there are no viable options:
         └─ chainsaw 0.2.5 | 0.2.6 | 0.2.7 | 0.2.8 | 0.2.9 | 0.2.10 | 0.2.11 | 0.2.12 | 0.2.13 | 0.2.14 is excluded because the package is uploaded after the cutoff date of 2025-04-08 04:56:48.943953
      UT
```

### Issue description

The `workspace.exclude-newer` overrides the channel version, which I believe to be wrong.

### Expected behavior

It should be `workspace.exclude-newer` > `workspace.channels.exclude-newer` > `[(pypi-)exclude-newer]` IMO.

</pr_description>

    29	/// A trait that implement various methods for collections that combine
    30	/// attributes of Features It is implemented by Environment, GroupedEnvironment
    31	/// and SolveGroup. Remove some of the boilerplate of combining features and its
    32	/// derived data from multiple sources.
    33	///
    34	/// The name of the lifetime parameter is named `'source` that the borrow comes
    35	/// from the source of the data for most implementations this will be the pixi
    36	/// project.
    37	///
    38	/// There is blanket implementation available for all types that implement
    39	/// [`HasWorkspaceManifest`] and [`HasFeaturesIter`]
    40	pub trait FeaturesExt<'source>: HasWorkspaceManifest<'source> + HasFeaturesIter<'source> {
    41	    /// Returns the channels associated with this collection, preserving the
    42	    /// effective metadata for the first winning entry of every unique channel.
    43	    fn prioritized_channels(
    44	        &self,
    45	    ) -> IndexMap<&'source NamedChannelOrUrl, &'source PrioritizedChannel> {
    46	        let channels = self.features().flat_map(|feature| match &feature.channels {
    47	            Some(channels) => channels,
    48	            None => &self.workspace_manifest().workspace.channels,
    49	        });
    50	
    51	        let mut prioritized = IndexMap::new();
    52	        for channel in channels.into_iter().sorted_by(|a, b| {
    53	            let a = a.priority.unwrap_or(0);
    54	            let b = b.priority.unwrap_or(0);
    55	            b.cmp(&a)
    56	        }) {
    57	            prioritized.entry(&channel.channel).or_insert(channel);
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        prioritized
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    /// Returns the channels associated with this collection.
    64	    ///
    65	    /// Users can specify custom channels on a per-feature basis. This method
    66	    /// collects and deduplicates all the channels from all the features in
    67	    /// the order they are defined in the manifest.
    68	    ///
    69	    /// If a feature does not specify any channel the default channels from the
    70	    /// project metadata are used instead.
    71	    fn channels(&self) -> IndexSet<&'source NamedChannelOrUrl> {
    72	        self.prioritized_channels().into_keys().collect()
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    /// Returns the channels associated with this collection.
    76	    ///
    77	    /// This function is similar to [`Self::channels]` but it resolves the
    78	    /// channel urls using the provided channel config.
    79	    fn channel_urls(
    80	        &self,
    81	        channel_config: &ChannelConfig,
    82	    ) -> Result<Vec<ChannelUrl>, ParseChannelError> {
    83	        self.channels()
    84	            .into_iter()
    85	            .cloned()
    86	            .map(|channel| channel.into_base_url(channel_config))
    87	            .collect()
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    /// Returns the channel priority, error on multiple, different values, return None if
    91	    /// no value is set.
    92	    ///
    93	    /// When using multiple channel priorities over different features we should
    94	    /// error as the user should decide what they want.
    95	    fn channel_priority(&self) -> Result<Option<ChannelPriority>, ChannelPriorityCombinationError> {
    96	        let mut channel_priority = None;
    97	        for feature in self.features() {
    98	            if let Some(priority) = feature.channel_priority {
    99	                // If we already have a priority and it's different, error
   100	                if channel_priority.is_some() && channel_priority != Some(priority) {
   101	                    return Err(ChannelPriorityCombinationError);
   102	                }
   103	                channel_priority = Some(priority);
   104	            }
   105	        }
   106	        Ok(channel_priority)
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    /// Returns the raw workspace exclude-newer configuration before channel and
   110	    /// package-specific overrides are applied.
   111	    fn exclude_newer_raw(&self) -> Option<ExcludeNewer> {
   112	        self.workspace_manifest().workspace.exclude_newer
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    /// Returns the effective exclude-newer solver configuration.
   116	    fn exclude_newer_config(
   117	        &self,
   118	    ) -> Result<Option<rattler_solve::ExcludeNewer>, ParseChannelError> {
   119	        self.exclude_newer_config_resolved()
   120	            .map(|exclude_newer| exclude_newer.map(Into::into))
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    /// Returns the effective exclude-newer solver configuration with absolute cutoffs.
   124	    fn exclude_newer_config_resolved(
   125	        &self,
   126	    ) -> Result<Option<ResolvedExcludeNewer>, ParseChannelError> {
   127	        let mut exclude_newer = self
   128	            .exclude_newer_raw()
   129	            .map(|config| ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(config.cutoff()));
   130	
   131	        for channel in self.prioritized_channels().into_values() {
   132	            let Some(channel_exclude_newer) = channel.exclude_newer else {
   133	                continue;
   134	            };
   135	
   136	            let config = exclude_newer.get_or_insert_with(|| {
   137	                ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(DateTime::<Utc>::MAX_UTC)
   138	            });
   139	
   140	            *config = match channel_exclude_newer {
   141	                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => config
   142	                    .clone()
   143	                    .with_channel_cutoff(channel.channel.to_string(), dt),
   144	                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => config.clone().with_channel_cutoff(
   145	                    channel.channel.to_string(),
   146	                    ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration).cutoff(),
   147	                ),
   148	            };
   149	        }
   150	
   151	        for (name, package_exclude_newer) in &self
   152	            .workspace_manifest()
   153	            .workspace
   154	            .exclude_newer_package_overrides
   155	        {
   156	            let config = exclude_newer.get_or_insert_with(|| {
   157	                ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(DateTime::<Utc>::MAX_UTC)
   158	            });
   159	
   160	            *config = match package_exclude_newer {
   161	                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => {
   162	                    config.clone().with_package_cutoff(name.clone(), *dt)
   163	                }
   164	                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => config
   165	                    .clone()
   166	                    .with_package_cutoff(name.clone(), ExcludeNewer::Duration(*duration).cutoff()),
   167	            };
   168	        }
   169	
   170	        Ok(exclude_newer)
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    /// Returns the effective PyPI exclude-newer solver configuration with absolute cutoffs.
   174	    fn pypi_exclude_newer_config_resolved(&self) -> ResolvedPypiExcludeNewer {
   175	        let mut exclude_newer = self
   176	            .exclude_newer_raw()
   177	            .map(|config| ResolvedPypiExcludeNewer::from_datetime(config.cutoff()))
   178	            .unwrap_or_default();
   179	
   180	        for (name, package_exclude_newer) in &self
   181	            .workspace_manifest()
   182	            .workspace
   183	            .pypi_exclude_newer_package_overrides
   184	        {
   185	            exclude_newer = match package_exclude_newer {
   186	                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => {
   187	                    exclude_newer.with_package_cutoff(name.as_normalized().clone(), *dt)
   188	                }
   189	                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => exclude_newer.with_package_cutoff(
   190	                    name.as_normalized().clone(),
   191	                    ExcludeNewer::Duration(*duration).cutoff(),
   192	                ),
   193	            };
   194	        }
   195	
   196	        exclude_newer
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    /// Returns the strategy for solving packages.
   200	    ///
   201	    /// The chosen strategy is the first explicitly declared one in a feature
   202	    /// as they are provided by the [`HasFeaturesIter::features`] iterator.
   203	    ///
   204	    /// If no feature declares a strategy, the default value of [`SolveStrategy`] is used.
   205	    fn solve_strategy(&self) -> SolveStrategy {
   206	        self.features()
   207	            .flat_map(|feature| feature.solve_strategy)
   208	            .next()
   209	            .unwrap_or_default()
   210	    }
   211	
   212	    /// Returns the platforms that this collection is compatible with.
   213	    ///
   214	    /// Which platforms a collection support depends on which platforms the
   215	    /// selected features of the collection supports. The platforms that are
   216	    /// supported by the collection is the intersection of the platforms
   217	    /// supported by its features.
   218	    ///
   219	    /// Features can specify which platforms they support through the
   220	    /// `platforms` key. If a feature does not specify any platforms the
   221	    /// features defined by the project are used.
   222	    fn platforms(&self) -> HashSet<Platform> {
   223	        self.features()
   224	            .map(|feature| {
   225	                match &feature.platforms {
   226	                    Some(platforms) => platforms,
   227	                    None => &self.workspace_manifest().workspace.platforms,
   228	                }
   229	                .iter()
   230	                .copied()
   231	                .collect::<HashSet<_>>()
   232	            })
   233	            .reduce(|accumulated_platforms, feat| {
   234	                accumulated_platforms.intersection(&feat).copied().collect()
   235	            })
   236	            .unwrap_or_default()
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    /// Returns the system requirements for this collection.
   240	    ///

     2	use rattler_conda_types::PackageName;
     3	use std::{collections::BTreeMap, str::FromStr};
     4	
     5	/// Specifies how to exclude newer packages from the solve.
     6	///
     7	/// Can be either:
     8	/// - An absolute timestamp
     9	/// - A relative duration (e.g., `7d`, `1h`, `30m`, `1h30m`)
    10	#[derive(Debug, Copy, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
    11	pub enum ExcludeNewer {
    12	    /// An absolute point in time. Packages newer than this are excluded.
    13	    Timestamp(DateTime<Utc>),
    14	    /// A relative duration. At solve time, packages newer than `now - duration`
    15	    /// are excluded.
    16	    Duration(std::time::Duration),
    17	}
    18	
    19	/// A fully resolved exclude-newer configuration with absolute cutoffs.
    20	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
    21	#[serde(rename_all = "kebab-case")]
    22	pub struct ResolvedExcludeNewer {
    23	    /// The default cutoff date. Packages uploaded after this date are excluded.
    24	    pub cutoff: DateTime<Utc>,
    25	
    26	    /// Channel-specific cutoff dates that override [`Self::cutoff`] for
    27	    /// records from matching channels.
    28	    #[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = "BTreeMap::is_empty")]
    29	    pub channel_cutoffs: BTreeMap<String, DateTime<Utc>>,
    30	
    31	    /// Package-specific cutoff dates that override both [`Self::cutoff`] and
    32	    /// [`Self::channel_cutoffs`] for matching package names.
    33	    #[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = "BTreeMap::is_empty")]
    34	    pub package_cutoffs: BTreeMap<PackageName, DateTime<Utc>>,
    35	
    36	    /// Whether to include packages that don't have a timestamp.
    37	    #[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = "std::ops::Not::not")]
    38	    pub include_unknown_timestamp: bool,
    39	}
    40	
    41	impl ExcludeNewer {
    42	    /// Returns the effective cutoff for the current time.
    43	    pub fn cutoff(&self) -> DateTime<Utc> {
    44	        match self {
    45	            Self::Timestamp(cutoff) => *cutoff,
    46	            Self::Duration(duration) => {
    47	                let duration = chrono::Duration::from_std(*duration)
    48	                    .expect("exclude-newer duration is too large");
    49	                Utc::now() - duration
    50	            }
    51	        }
    52	    }
    53	}
    54	
    55	impl ResolvedExcludeNewer {
    56	    /// Creates a new configuration from an absolute cutoff date.
    57	    pub fn from_datetime(cutoff: DateTime<Utc>) -> Self {
    58	        Self {
    59	            cutoff,
    60	            channel_cutoffs: BTreeMap::new(),
    61	            package_cutoffs: BTreeMap::new(),
    62	            include_unknown_timestamp: false,
    63	        }
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    /// Adds a channel-specific cutoff override.
    67	    pub fn with_channel_cutoff(
    68	        mut self,
    69	        channel: impl Into<String>,
    70	        cutoff: DateTime<Utc>,
    71	    ) -> Self {
    72	        self.channel_cutoffs.insert(channel.into(), cutoff);
    73	        self
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    /// Adds a package-specific cutoff override.
    77	    pub fn with_package_cutoff(mut self, package: PackageName, cutoff: DateTime<Utc>) -> Self {
    78	        self.package_cutoffs.insert(package, cutoff);
    79	        self
    80	    }
    81	}
    82	
    83	impl From<ResolvedExcludeNewer> for rattler_solve::ExcludeNewer {
    84	    fn from(value: ResolvedExcludeNewer) -> Self {
    85	        let mut config = rattler_solve::ExcludeNewer::from_datetime(value.cutoff)
    86	            .with_include_unknown_timestamp(value.include_unknown_timestamp);
    87	
    88	        for (channel, cutoff) in value.channel_cutoffs {
    89	            config = config.with_channel_cutoff(channel, cutoff);
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        for (package, cutoff) in value.package_cutoffs {
    93	            config = config.with_package_cutoff(package, cutoff);
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        config
    97	    }
    98	}

   102

   302

docs/security.md:42:Use [`exclude-newer`](reference/pixi_manifest.md#exclude-newer-optional) to put a short delay on packages from public channels by default, then carve out exceptions only for artifacts you control or urgent security fixes that you have explicitly reviewed. This is a practical defense against compromised releases, rushed hostile uploads, or ecosystem incidents where a bad package is published and only detected shortly afterwards.

docs/security.md:82:This is how you respond when a vulnerable version is already known, especially if transitive dependency bounds would otherwise keep you stuck on an affected release. Overrides let you force dependency requirements during resolution so the solver can select a safe version even if upstream packages have not caught up yet. They are complementary to `exclude-newer`: `exclude-newer` reduces exposure to newly uploaded artifacts, while constraints, the `[exclude-newer]` tables, and overrides help you respond once a vulnerable version is already known.

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/docs/reference/pixi_manifest.md:
   293	### `exclude-newer` (optional)
   294	
   295	When specified on the workspace this will exclude any package from consideration that is newer than the specified timestamp or duration.
   296	This is useful to reproduce installations regardless of new package releases, or to reduce the risk of
   297	installing recently published (and potentially compromised) packages.
   298	
   299	The value may be specified in the following formats:
   300	
   301	* As an [RFC 3339](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc3339.html) timestamp (e.g. `2023-10-01T00:00:00Z`)
   302	* As a date in `YYYY-MM-DD` format (e.g. `2026-03-30`). This is interpreted as the start of the following day in UTC, so `2026-03-30` means `2026-03-31T00:00:00Z`.
   303	* As a relative duration (e.g. `7days`, `1h30m`, `30m`). The duration is relative to the current time at solve time.
   304	
   305	When using a relative duration, the lock file will be re-solved when a package is not included in the cutoff date.
   306	
   307	Both PyPi and conda packages are considered.
   308	
   309	For conda packages, the workspace-level cutoff can be overridden per package in the
   310	[`[exclude-newer]`](#exclude-newer-optional) table.
   311	
   312	For PyPI packages, the workspace-level cutoff can be overridden per package in the
   313	[`[pypi-exclude-newer]`](#exclude-newer-optional) table.
   314	
   315	This is especially useful when a package is pinned to a separate `channel` or `index` and needs a
   316	different cutoff than the rest of the workspace.
   317	
   318	```toml
   319	[workspace]
   320	exclude-newer = "2025-01-01"
   321	
   322	[dependencies]
   323	pytorch-cpu = { version = ">=2.10.0", channel = "pytorch" }
   324	
   325	[exclude-newer]
   326	pytorch-cpu = "0 days"
   327	openssl = "0 days"
   328	
   329	[pypi-dependencies]
   330	torch = { version = ">=2.10.0", index = "https://download.pytorch.org/whl/cu124" }
   331	
   332	[pypi-exclude-newer]
   333	torch = "0 days"
   334	```
   335	
   336	!!! note
   337	    Note that for Pypi package indexes the package index must support the `upload-time` field as specified in [`PEP 700`](https://peps.python.org/pep-0700/).
   338	    If the field is not present for a given distribution, the distribution will be treated as unavailable. PyPI provides `upload-time` for all packages.
   339	
   340	### `build-variants` (optional)

    90	/// time window (often within an hour). By requiring packages to have been
    91	/// published for a minimum duration, you give the community time to identify
    92	/// and report malicious packages before they can be installed.
    93	///
    94	/// This is similar to pnpm's `minimumReleaseAge` feature.
    95	///
    96	/// # Example
    97	///
    98	/// ```
    99	/// use std::time::Duration;
   100	/// use rattler_solve::ExcludeNewer;
   101	///
   102	/// // Only allow packages that have been published for at least 1 hour
   103	/// let config = ExcludeNewer::from_duration(Duration::from_secs(60 * 60))
   104	///     // But allow "my-internal-package" to use a package-specific cutoff
   105	///     .with_package_duration("my-internal-package".parse().unwrap(), Duration::ZERO)
   106	///     // And allow a trusted internal channel to skip the delay entirely
   107	///     .with_channel_duration("my-internal-channel", Duration::ZERO);
   108	/// ```
   109	#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]
   110	pub struct ExcludeNewer {
   111	    /// The default cutoff date. Packages uploaded after this date are excluded.
   112	    cutoff: DateTime<Utc>,
   113	
   114	    /// Channel-specific cutoff dates that override [`Self::cutoff`] for
   115	    /// records from matching channels.
   116	    ///
   117	    /// The key is matched against [`RepoDataRecord::channel`] exactly.
   118	    channel_cutoffs: HashMap<String, DateTime<Utc>>,
   119	
   120	    /// Package-specific cutoff dates that override both [`Self::cutoff`] and
   121	    /// [`Self::channel_cutoffs`] for matching package names.
   122	    package_cutoffs: HashMap<PackageName, DateTime<Utc>>,
   123	
   124	    /// Whether to include packages that don't have a timestamp.
   125	    include_unknown_timestamp: bool,
   126	}
   127	
   128	impl ExcludeNewer {
   129	    fn cutoff_from_duration(duration: std::time::Duration, now: DateTime<Utc>) -> DateTime<Utc> {
   130	        let duration =
   131	            chrono::Duration::from_std(duration).expect("exclude_newer duration is too large");
   132	        now - duration
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    /// Creates a new configuration from an absolute cutoff date.
   136	    pub fn from_datetime(cutoff: DateTime<Utc>) -> Self {
   137	        Self {
   138	            cutoff,
   139	            channel_cutoffs: HashMap::new(),
   140	            package_cutoffs: HashMap::new(),
   141	            include_unknown_timestamp: false,
   142	        }
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    /// Creates a new configuration from a relative duration.
   146	    pub fn from_duration(duration: std::time::Duration) -> Self {
   147	        Self::from_duration_with_now(duration, Utc::now())
   148	    }
   149	
   150	    /// Creates a new configuration from a relative duration and explicit
   151	    /// reference time.
   152	    pub fn from_duration_with_now(duration: std::time::Duration, now: DateTime<Utc>) -> Self {
   153	        Self {
   154	            cutoff: Self::cutoff_from_duration(duration, now),
   155	            channel_cutoffs: HashMap::new(),
   156	            package_cutoffs: HashMap::new(),
   157	            include_unknown_timestamp: false,
   158	        }
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    /// Sets the absolute cutoff override for a specific package.
   162	    pub fn with_package_cutoff(mut self, package: PackageName, cutoff: DateTime<Utc>) -> Self {
   163	        self.package_cutoffs.insert(package, cutoff);
   164	        self
   165	    }
   166	
   167	    /// Sets the duration override for a specific package.
   168	    pub fn with_package_duration(
   169	        mut self,
   170	        package: PackageName,

   240	    /// Computes the cutoff time for the given package and channel.
   241	    pub fn cutoff_for_package(
   242	        &self,
   243	        package: &PackageName,
   244	        channel: Option<&str>,
   245	    ) -> DateTime<Utc> {
   246	        self.package_cutoffs
   247	            .get(package)
   248	            .copied()
   249	            .or_else(|| channel.and_then(|channel| self.channel_cutoffs.get(channel).copied()))
   250	            .unwrap_or(self.cutoff)
   251	    }
   252	
   253	    /// Returns whether a package should be excluded.
   254	    pub fn is_excluded(
   255	        &self,
   256	        package: &PackageName,
   257	        channel: Option<&str>,
   258	        timestamp: Option<&TimestampMs>,
   259	    ) -> bool {
   260	        match timestamp {
   261	            Some(timestamp) => *timestamp > self.cutoff_for_package(package, channel),
   262	            None => !self.include_unknown_timestamp(),
   263	        }
   264	    }
   265	}

   269	        Self::from_datetime(value)
   270	    }
   271	}

    21	
    22	/// Contains all information that describes the input of a conda environment.
    23	/// All information about both binary and source packages is stored in the
    24	/// specification, when solving this information is passed to the solver,
    25	/// and the result is returned.
    26	///
    27	/// Unlike [`super::PixiEnvironmentSpec`], solving a `SolveCondaEnvironmentSpec`
    28	/// instance does not require any recursive calls since all information is
    29	/// already available in the specification.
    30	#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize)]
    31	#[serde(rename_all = "kebab-case")]
    32	pub struct SolveCondaEnvironmentSpec {
    33	    /// A name, useful for debugging purposes.
    34	    pub name: Option<String>,
    35	
    36	    /// Requirements on source packages.
    37	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "DependencyMap::is_empty")]
    38	    pub source_specs: DependencyMap<rattler_conda_types::PackageName, SourceSpec>,
    39	
    40	    /// Requirements on binary packages.
    41	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "DependencyMap::is_empty")]
    42	    pub binary_specs: DependencyMap<rattler_conda_types::PackageName, BinarySpec>,
    43	
    44	    /// Additional constraints of the environment
    45	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "DependencyMap::is_empty")]
    46	    pub constraints: DependencyMap<rattler_conda_types::PackageName, BinarySpec>,
    47	
    48	    /// Dev source records whose dependencies should be installed.
    49	    #[serde(skip)]
    50	    pub dev_source_records: Vec<pixi_record::DevSourceRecord>,
    51	
    52	    /// Available source repodata records.
    53	    #[serde(skip)]
    54	    pub source_repodata: Vec<Arc<SourceMetadata>>,
    55	
    56	    /// Available Binary repodata records.
    57	    #[serde(skip)]
    58	    pub binary_repodata: Vec<RepoData>,
    59	
    60	    /// The records of the packages that are currently already installed. These
    61	    /// are used as hints to reduce the difference between individual solves.
    62	    #[serde(skip)]
    63	    pub installed: Vec<PixiRecord>,
    64	
    65	    /// The platform to solve for
    66	    pub platform: Platform,
    67	
    68	    /// The channels to use for solving
    69	    pub channels: Vec<ChannelUrl>,
    70	
    71	    /// The virtual packages to include in the solve
    72	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Vec::is_empty")]
    73	    pub virtual_packages: Vec<GenericVirtualPackage>,
    74	
    75	    /// The strategy to use for solving
    76	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "crate::is_default")]
    77	    pub strategy: SolveStrategy,
    78	
    79	    /// The priority of channels to use for solving
    80	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "crate::is_default")]
    81	    pub channel_priority: ChannelPriority,
    82	
    83	    /// Exclude packages newer than the configured default and per-channel cutoffs.
    84	    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]
    85	    pub exclude_newer: Option<ResolvedExcludeNewer>,
    86	
    87	    /// The channel configuration to use for this environment.
    88	    pub channel_config: ChannelConfig,
    89	}
    90	
    91	impl Default for SolveCondaEnvironmentSpec {
    92	    fn default() -> Self {
    93	        Self {
    94	            name: None,
    95	            source_specs: DependencyMap::default(),
    96	            binary_specs: DependencyMap::default(),
    97	            constraints: DependencyMap::default(),
    98	            dev_source_records: vec![],
    99	            source_repodata: vec![],
   100	            binary_repodata: vec![],
   101	            installed: vec![],
   102	            platform: Platform::current(),
   103	            channels: vec![],
   104	            virtual_packages: vec![],
   105	            strategy: SolveStrategy::default(),
   106	            channel_priority: ChannelPriority::default(),
   107	            exclude_newer: None,
   108	            channel_config: ChannelConfig::default_with_root_dir(PathBuf::from(".")),
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	}
   112	
   113	impl SolveCondaEnvironmentSpec {
   114	    /// Solves this environment
   115	    pub async fn solve(
   116	        self,
   117	    ) -> Result<Vec<PixiRecord>, CommandDispatcherError<SolveCondaEnvironmentError>> {
   118	        // Solving is a CPU-intensive task, we spawn this on a background task to allow
   119	        // for more concurrency.
   120	        let solve_result = tokio::task::spawn_blocking(move || {
   121	            let exclude_newer = self.exclude_newer.clone().map(Into::into);
   122	
   123	            // Determine for which records we have source records because those records should only
   124	            //  be installed as source records.
   125	            let package_names_from_source = self
   126	                .source_repodata
   127	                .iter()
   128	                .flat_map(|metadata| &metadata.records)
   129	                .map(|metadata| &metadata.package_record.name)
   130	                .dedup()
   131	                .collect::<HashSet<_>>();
   132	
   133	            // Filter all installed packages
   134	            let installed = self
   135	                .installed
   136	                .into_iter()
   137	                // Only lock binary records
   138	                .filter_map(|record| record.into_binary())
   139	                // Filter any record we want as a source record
   140	                .filter(|record| !package_names_from_source.contains(&record.package_record.name))
   141	                .collect();
   142	
   143	            // Create direct dependencies on the source packages to feed to the solver.
   144	            let source_match_specs = self
   145	                .source_specs
   146	                .into_specs()
   147	                .map(|(name, spec)| {
   148	                    MatchSpec::from_nameless(spec.to_nameless_match_spec(), name.into())
   149	                })
   150	                .collect::<Vec<_>>();

   236	                                    .unwrap_or_default();
   237	                                MatchSpec::from_nameless(nameless, name.clone().into()).to_string()
   238	                            })
   239	                            .collect(),
   240	                        constrains: dev_source
   241	                            .constraints
   242	                            .iter_specs()
   243	                            .filter(|(name, _)| !dev_source_names.contains(*name))
   244	                            .filter_map(|(name, spec)| {
   245	                                let nameless = spec
   246	                                    .clone()
   247	                                    .try_into_nameless_match_spec(&self.channel_config)
   248	                                    .ok()?;
   249	                                Some(
   250	                                    MatchSpec::from_nameless(nameless, name.clone().into())
   251	                                        .to_string(),
   252	                                )
   253	                            })
   254	                            .collect(),
   255	                        ..rattler_conda_types::PackageRecord::new(
   256	                            rattler_conda_types::PackageName::new_unchecked(prefixed_name.clone()),
   257	                            Version::major(0),
   258	                            build_string.clone(),
   259	                        )
   260	                    },
   261	                    url: url.clone(),
   262	                    identifier: DistArchiveIdentifier {
   263	                        identifier: ArchiveIdentifier {
   264	                            name: prefixed_name.clone(),
   265	                            version: "0".to_string(),
   266	                            build_string: format!("{build_string}_devsource"),
   267	                        },
   268	                        archive_type: CondaArchiveType::Conda.into(),
   269	                    },
   270	                    channel: None,
   271	                };
   272	                url_to_dev_source.insert(url, (dev_source, repodata_record));
   273	            }
   274	
   275	            // Collect repodata records from the remote servers, source metadata, and dev sources
   276	            // together. The source and dev source records go into the first "channel" to ensure
   277	            // they are picked first.
   278	            //
   279	            // TODO: This only holds up when the channel priority is strict. We should
   280	            // probably enforce this better somehow..
   281	            let mut solvable_records = Vec::with_capacity(self.binary_repodata.len() + 1);
   282	            solvable_records.push(
   283	                url_to_source_package
   284	                    .values()
   285	                    .map(|(_, record)| record)
   286	                    .chain(url_to_dev_source.values().map(|(_, record)| record))
   287	                    .collect_vec(),
   288	            );
   289	            for repo_data in &self.binary_repodata {
   290	                solvable_records.push(repo_data.iter().collect_vec());
   291	            }
   292	
   293	            // Construct a solver task that we can start solving.
   294	            let task = rattler_solve::SolverTask {
   295	                specs: source_match_specs
   296	                    .into_iter()
   297	                    .chain(binary_match_specs)
   298	                    .chain(dev_source_match_specs)
   299	                    .collect(),
   300	                locked_packages: installed,
   301	                virtual_packages: self.virtual_packages,
   302	                channel_priority: self.channel_priority,
   303	                exclude_newer,
   304	                strategy: self.strategy,
   305	                constraints: constrains_match_specs,
   306	                ..rattler_solve::SolverTask::from_iter(solvable_records)
   307	            };
   308	
   309	            let solver_result = rattler_solve::resolvo::Solver.solve(task)?;
   310	
   311	            // Convert the results back into pixi records.
   312	            Ok::<_, SolveCondaEnvironmentError>(
   313	                solver_result
   314	                    .records
   315	                    .into_iter()
   316	                    .filter_map(|record| {
   317	                        if let Some(source_record) = url_to_source_package.remove(&record.url) {
   318	                            // This is a source package, we want to return the source record
   319	                            // instead of the binary record.
   320	                            return Some(PixiRecord::Source(source_record.0.clone()));
   321	                        } else if let Some(_dev_source) = url_to_dev_source.remove(&record.url) {
   322	                            // This is a dev source, we don't want to return it.
   323	                            return None;
   324	                        }
   325	
   326	                        Some(PixiRecord::Binary(record))
   327	                    })
   328	                    .collect_vec(),
   329	            )
   330	        })
   331	        .await;
   332	
   333	        // Error out if the background task failed or was canceled.
   334	        match solve_result.map_err(JoinError::try_into_panic) {
   335	            Err(Err(_)) => Err(CommandDispatcherError::Cancelled),
   336	            Err(Ok(panic)) => std::panic::resume_unwind(panic),
   337	            Ok(Err(err)) => Err(CommandDispatcherError::Failed(err)),
   338	            Ok(Ok(result)) => Ok(result),
   339	        }
   340	    }

   135	        self,
   136	        command_queue: CommandDispatcher,
   137	        gateway_reporter: Option<Box<dyn rattler_repodata_gateway::Reporter>>,
   138	    ) -> Result<Vec<PixiRecord>, CommandDispatcherError<SolvePixiEnvironmentError>> {
   139	        // Process dev sources to get their metadata (before dependencies are moved)
   140	        let dev_source_records = self.process_dev_sources(&command_queue).await?;
   141	
   142	        let exclude_newer = self.exclude_newer.clone();
   143	
   144	        // Split the requirements into source and binary requirements.
   145	        let (dev_source_source_specs, dev_source_binary_specs) =
   146	            DevSourceRecord::split_into_source_and_binary_requirements(

   152	            );
   153	
   154	        Self::check_missing_channels(binary_specs.clone(), &self.channels, &self.channel_config)
   155	            .map_err(|err| CommandDispatcherError::Failed(*err))?;
   156	
   157	        // Recursively collect the metadata of all the source specs.
   158	        let CollectedSourceMetadata {
   159	            source_repodata,
   160	            transitive_dependencies,
   161	        } = SourceMetadataCollector::new(
   162	            command_queue.clone(),

   164	            self.channel_config.clone(),

   172	        .collect(
   173	            source_specs
   174	                .iter_specs()
   175	                .map(|(name, spec)| (name.clone(), spec.clone()))
   176	                .chain(dev_source_source_specs.into_specs()),
   177	        )
   178	        .await
   179	        .map_err_with(SolvePixiEnvironmentError::from)?;
   180	
   181	        // Convert the binary specs into match specs as well.
   182	        let binary_match_specs = binary_specs
   183	            .clone()
   184	            .into_match_specs(&self.channel_config)
   185	            .map_err(SolvePixiEnvironmentError::from)
   186	            .map_err(CommandDispatcherError::Failed)?;
   187

   192

   194	        // direct dependencies of the environment and the direct dependencies of

   197	        let fetch_repodata_start = Instant::now();
   198	        let query = command_queue

   221	        tracing::debug!(

   223	            fetch_repodata_start.elapsed()
   224	        );
   225	
   226	        // Construct a solver specification from the collected metadata and solve the
   227	        // environment.
   228	        command_queue
   229	            .solve_conda_environment(SolveCondaEnvironmentSpec {
   230	                name: self.name,
   231	                source_specs,
   232	                binary_specs,
   233	                constraints: self.constraints,
   234	                dev_source_records,

   241	                strategy: self.strategy,
   242	                channel_priority: self.channel_priority,
   243	                exclude_newer,
   244	                channel_config: self.channel_config,
   245	            })
   246	            .await
   247	            .map_err_with(SolvePixiEnvironmentError::from)
   248	    }

     1	use std::sync::Arc;
     2	
     3	use rattler_conda_types::RepoDataRecord;
     4	
     5	/// A container for [`RepoDataRecord`]s that are returned from the [`super::Gateway`].
     6	///
     7	/// Records are stored as `Arc<RepoDataRecord>` so that cloning is cheap
     8	/// (reference count bump rather than deep copy).
     9	///
    10	/// `RepoData` uses internal reference counting, therefor it is relatively
    11	/// cheap to clone.
    12	#[derive(Debug, Default, Clone)]
    13	pub struct RepoData {
    14	    pub(crate) records: Vec<Arc<RepoDataRecord>>,
    15	}
    16	
    17	impl RepoData {
    18	    /// Returns an iterator over all the records in this instance.
    19	    pub fn iter(&self) -> RepoDataIterator<'_> {
    20	        RepoDataIterator {
    21	            inner: self.records.iter(),
    22	        }
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    /// Returns the total number of records stored in this instance.
    26	    pub fn len(&self) -> usize {
    27	        self.records.len()
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    /// Returns true if there are no records stored in this instance.
    31	    pub fn is_empty(&self) -> bool {
    32	        self.records.is_empty()
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    /// Returns an iterator over the Arc-wrapped records.
    36	    ///
    37	    /// This is useful when you want to clone records cheaply (Arc clone
    38	    /// instead of deep copy).
    39	    pub fn iter_arc(&self) -> impl ExactSizeIterator<Item = &Arc<RepoDataRecord>> {
    40	        self.records.iter()
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    /// Returns true if there is at least one [`RepoDataRecord`] with
    44	    /// [`rattler_conda_types::package::RunExportsJson`] missing.
    45	    pub fn is_run_exports_missing(&self) -> bool {
    46	        self.iter().any(|r| r.package_record.run_exports.is_none())
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    /// Returns number of missing run exports from the underlying
    50	    /// [`RepoDataRecord`]s.
    51	    pub fn run_exports_missing(&self) -> usize {
    52	        self.iter()
    53	            .filter(|r| r.package_record.run_exports.is_none())
    54	            .count()
    55	    }
    56	}
    57	
    58	impl<'r> IntoIterator for &'r RepoData {
    59	    type Item = &'r RepoDataRecord;
    60	    type IntoIter = RepoDataIterator<'r>;
    61	
    62	    fn into_iter(self) -> Self::IntoIter {
    63	        self.iter()
    64	    }
    65	}
    66	
    67	/// An iterator over the records in a [`RepoData`] instance.
    68	pub struct RepoDataIterator<'r> {
    69	    inner: std::slice::Iter<'r, Arc<RepoDataRecord>>,
    70	}
    71	
    72	impl<'r> Iterator for RepoDataIterator<'r> {
    73	    type Item = &'r RepoDataRecord;
    74	
    75	    fn next(&mut self) -> Option<Self::Item> {
    76	        self.inner.next().map(std::convert::AsRef::as_ref)
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    fn size_hint(&self) -> (usize, Option<usize>) {
    80	        self.inner.size_hint()
    81	    }
    82	}
    83	
    84	impl std::iter::FusedIterator for RepoDataIterator<'_> {}
    85	
    86	impl ExactSizeIterator for RepoDataIterator<'_> {
    87	    fn len(&self) -> usize {
    88	        self.inner.len()
    89	    }

     7	
     8	/// Represents a channel base url. This is a wrapper around an url that is
     9	/// normalized:
    10	///
    11	/// * The URL always contains a trailing `/`.
    12	///
    13	/// This is useful to be able to compare different channels.
    14	#[derive(Clone, Hash, Eq, PartialEq, Deserialize)]
    15	#[serde(transparent)]
    16	pub struct ChannelUrl(UrlWithTrailingSlash);
    17	
    18	impl ChannelUrl {
    19	    /// Returns the base Url of the channel.
    20	    pub fn url(&self) -> &UrlWithTrailingSlash {
    21	        &self.0
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    /// Returns the string representation of the url.
    25	    pub fn as_str(&self) -> &str {
    26	        self.0.as_str()
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    /// Append the platform to the base url.
    30	    pub fn platform_url(&self, platform: Platform) -> Url {
    31	        self.0
    32	            .join(&format!("{}/", platform.as_str())) // trailing slash is important here as this signifies a directory
    33	            .expect("platform is a valid url fragment")
    34	    }
    35	}
    36	
    37	// Override the behavior of the `Serialize` trait to remove the trailing slash.
    38	// In code, we want to ensure that a trailing slash is always present but when
    39	// we serialize the type it can be removed to safe space and make it look better
    40	// for humans.
    41	impl Serialize for ChannelUrl {
    42	    fn serialize<S>(&self, serializer: S) -> Result<S::Ok, S::Error>
    43	    where
    44	        S: serde::Serializer,
    45	    {
    46	        self.as_str().trim_end_matches('/').serialize(serializer)

    52	        write!(f, "{}", self.0.as_str())
    53	    }
    54	}

    83	/// Represents a channel description as either a name (e.g. `conda-forge`) or a
    84	/// base url.
    85	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Eq, PartialEq, Hash)]
    86	pub enum NamedChannelOrUrl {
    87	    /// A named channel
    88	    Name(String),
    89	
    90	    /// A url
    91	    Url(Url),
    92	
    93	    /// A path. Can either be absolute or relative.
    94	    Path(Utf8TypedPathBuf),
    95	}
    96	
    97	impl NamedChannelOrUrl {
    98	    /// Returns the string representation of the channel.
    99	    ///
   100	    /// This method ensures that if the channel is a url, it does not end with a
   101	    /// `/`.
   102	    pub fn as_str(&self) -> &str {
   103	        match self {
   104	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Name(name) => name,
   105	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Url(url) => url.as_str().trim_end_matches('/'),
   106	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Path(path) => path.as_str(),
   107	        }
   108	    }
   109	
   110	    /// Converts the channel to a base url using the given configuration.
   111	    /// This method ensures that the base url always ends with a `/`.
   112	    pub fn into_base_url(self, config: &ChannelConfig) -> Result<ChannelUrl, ParseChannelError> {
   113	        let url = match self {
   114	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Name(name) => {
   115	                let mut base_url = config.channel_alias.clone();
   116	                if let Ok(mut segments) = base_url.path_segments_mut() {
   117	                    for segment in name.split(&['/', '\\']) {
   118	                        segments.push(segment);
   119	                    }
   120	                }
   121	                base_url.into()
   122	            }
   123	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Url(url) => url.into(),
   124	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Path(path) => {
   125	                let absolute_path = absolute_path(path.as_str(), &config.root_dir)?;
   126	                directory_path_to_url(absolute_path.to_path())
   127	                    .map_err(|_err| ParseChannelError::InvalidPath(path.to_string()))?
   128	                    .into()
   129	            }
   130	        };
   131	        Ok(url)
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    /// Converts this instance into a channel.
   135	    pub fn into_channel(self, config: &ChannelConfig) -> Result<Channel, ParseChannelError> {
   136	        let name = match &self {
   137	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Name(name) => Some(name.clone()),
   138	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Url(base_url) => config.strip_channel_alias(base_url),
   139	            NamedChannelOrUrl::Path(_) => None,
   140	        };
   141	        let base_url = self.into_base_url(config)?;
   142	        Ok(Channel {
   143	            name,
   144	            base_url,
   145	            platforms: None,

    63	impl CondaPrefixUpdaterBuilder<'_> {
    64	    /// Builds the conda prefix updater by extracting the necessary information
    65	    /// from the group.
    66	    pub fn finish(self) -> miette::Result<CondaPrefixUpdater> {
    67	        let channels = self
    68	            .group
    69	            .channel_urls(&self.group.workspace().channel_config())
    70	            .into_diagnostic()?;
    71	        let name = self.group.name();
    72	        let prefix = self.group.prefix();
    73	        let variant_config = self.group.workspace().variants(self.platform)?;
    74	        let exclude_newer = self
    75	            .group
    76	            .exclude_newer_config_resolved()
    77	            .into_diagnostic()?;
    78	
    79	        Ok(CondaPrefixUpdater::new(
    80	            channels,
    81	            self.group.channel_config(),
    82	            name,
    83	            prefix,
    84	            self.platform,
    85	            self.virtual_packages,
    86	            variant_config,
    87	            exclude_newer,
    88	            self.command_dispatcher,
    89	        ))
    90	    }

   124	fn fmt_channel_priority(priority: rattler_solve::ChannelPriority) -> &'static str {
   125	    match priority {
   126	        rattler_solve::ChannelPriority::Strict => "strict",
   127	        rattler_solve::ChannelPriority::Disabled => "disabled",
   128	    }
   129	}
   130	
   131	fn fmt_solve_strategy(strategy: rattler_solve::SolveStrategy) -> &'static str {
   132	    match strategy {
   133	        rattler_solve::SolveStrategy::Highest => "highest",
   134	        rattler_solve::SolveStrategy::LowestVersion => "lowest-version",
   135	        rattler_solve::SolveStrategy::LowestVersionDirect => "lowest-version-direct",
   136	    }
   137	}

   139	#[derive(Debug, Error)]
   140	pub struct ExcludeNewerMismatch {
   141	    package: String,
   142	    timestamp: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,
   143	    exclude_newer: chrono::DateTime<chrono::Utc>,
   144	}
   145	
   146	impl Display for ExcludeNewerMismatch {
   147	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
   148	        write!(
   149	            f,
   150	            "the locked package '{}' has timestamp {}, which is newer than the environment's exclude-newer cutoff {}",
   151	            self.package, self.timestamp, self.exclude_newer
   152	        )
   153	    }
   154	}
   155	
   156	fn verify_exclude_newer(
   157	    environment: &Environment<'_>,
   158	    locked_environment: &rattler_lock::Environment<'_>,
   159	) -> Result<(), ExcludeNewerMismatch> {
   160	    for (_platform, packages) in locked_environment.conda_packages_by_platform() {
   161	        let Some(exclude_newer) = environment
   162	            .exclude_newer_config()
   163	            .expect("environment channels were already validated")
   164	        else {
   165	            continue;
   166	        };
   167	
   168	        for package in packages {
   169	            let record = package.record();
   170	            let channel = package
   171	                .as_binary()
   172	                .and_then(|binary| binary.channel.as_ref())
   173	                .map(ToString::to_string);
   174	
   175	            if let Some(timestamp) = record.timestamp.as_ref()
   176	                && exclude_newer.is_excluded(&record.name, channel.as_deref(), Some(timestamp))
   177	            {
   178	                return Err(ExcludeNewerMismatch {
   179	                    package: record.name.as_source().to_string(),
   180	                    timestamp: (*timestamp).into(),
   181	                    exclude_newer: exclude_newer
   182	                        .cutoff_for_package(&record.name, channel.as_deref()),
   183	                });
   184	            }
   185	        }
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    Ok(())
   189	}

   206	            )

   209	                f,
   210	                "the indexes used to previously solve to lock file are missing"

   330	    /// Returns the environment variables that should be set when activating
   331	    /// this environment.
   332	    ///
   333	    /// The environment variables of all features are combined in the order they
   334	    /// are defined for the environment.
   335	    pub fn activation_env(&self, platform: Option<Platform>) -> IndexMap<String, String> {
   336	        self.features()
   337	            .map(|f| f.activation_env(platform))
   338	            .fold(IndexMap::new(), |mut acc, env| {
   339	                acc.extend(env.iter().map(|(k, v)| (k.clone(), v.clone())));
   340	                acc
   341	            })
   342	    }
   343	
   344	    /// Validates that the given platform is supported by this environment.
   345	    fn validate_platform_support(
   346	        &self,
   347	        platform: Option<Platform>,
   348	    ) -> Result<(), UnsupportedPlatformError> {
   349	        if let Some(platform) = platform
   350	            && !self.platforms().contains(&platform)
   351	        {
   352	            return Err(UnsupportedPlatformError {
   353	                environments_platforms: self.platforms().into_iter().collect(),
   354	                environment: self.name().clone(),
   355	                platform,
   356	            });
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        Ok(())
   360	    }

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /usr/local/cargo/registry/src/index.crates.io-1949cf8c6b5b557f/rattler_conda_types-0.44.4/src/channel/mod.rs:
    35	pub struct ChannelConfig {
    36	    /// A url to prefix to channel names that don't start with a Url. Usually
    37	    /// this Url refers to the `https://conda.anaconda.org` server but users are free to change this. This allows
    38	    /// naming channels just by their name instead of their entire Url (e.g.
    39	    /// "conda-forge" actually refers to `<https://conda.anaconda.org/conda-forge>`).
    40	    ///
    41	    /// The default value is: <https://conda.anaconda.org>
    42	    #[serde(alias = "channel_alias")] // Continue supporting snake_case alias
    43	    pub channel_alias: Url,
    44	
    45	    /// For local channels, the root directory from which to resolve relative
    46	    /// paths. Most of the time you would initialize this with the current
    47	    /// working directory.
    48	    #[serde(alias = "root_dir")] // Continue supporting snake_case alias
    49	    pub root_dir: PathBuf,
    50	}
    51	
    52	impl ChannelConfig {
    53	    /// Create a new `ChannelConfig` with the default values.
    54	    pub fn default_with_root_dir(root_dir: PathBuf) -> Self {
    55	        Self {
    56	            root_dir,
    57	            channel_alias: Url::from_str(DEFAULT_CHANNEL_ALIAS)
    58	                .expect("could not parse default channel alias"),
    59	        }
    60	    }
    61	    /// Strip the channel alias if the base url is "under" the channel alias.
    62	    /// This returns the name of the channel (for example "conda-forge" for
    63	    /// `https://conda.anaconda.org/conda-forge` when the channel alias is
    64	    /// `https://conda.anaconda.org`).
    65	    pub fn strip_channel_alias(&self, base_url: &Url) -> Option<String> {
    66	        base_url
    67	            .as_str()
    68	            .strip_prefix(self.channel_alias.as_str())
    69	            .map(|s| s.trim_matches('/').to_string())
    70	            .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    /// Returns the canonical name of a channel with the given base url.
    74	    pub fn canonical_name(&self, base_url: &Url) -> String {
    75	        if let Some(stripped) = self.strip_channel_alias(base_url) {
    76	            stripped
    77	        } else {
    78	            base_url.clone().redact().to_string()
    79	        }
    80	    }

    /// Returns the effective exclude-newer solver configuration with absolute cutoffs.
    fn exclude_newer_config_resolved(
        &self,
    ) -> Result<Option<ResolvedExcludeNewer>, ParseChannelError> {
        let mut exclude_newer = self
            .exclude_newer_raw()
            .map(|config| ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(config.cutoff()));

        for channel in self.prioritized_channels().into_values() {
            let Some(channel_exclude_newer) = channel.exclude_newer else {
                continue;
            };

            let config = exclude_newer.get_or_insert_with(|| {
                ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(DateTime::<Utc>::MAX_UTC)
            });

            *config = match channel_exclude_newer {
                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => config
                    .clone()
                    .with_channel_cutoff(channel.channel.to_string(), dt),
                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => config.clone().with_channel_cutoff(
                    channel.channel.to_string(),
                    ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration).cutoff(),
                ),
            };
        }

        for (name, package_exclude_newer) in &self
            .workspace_manifest()
            .workspace
            .exclude_newer_package_overrides
        {
            let config = exclude_newer.get_or_insert_with(|| {
                ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(DateTime::<Utc>::MAX_UTC)
            });

            *config = match package_exclude_newer {
                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => {
                    config.clone().with_package_cutoff(name.clone(), *dt)
                }
                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => config
                    .clone()
                    .with_package_cutoff(name.clone(), ExcludeNewer::Duration(*duration).cutoff()),
            };
        }

        Ok(exclude_newer)
    }

    /// Returns the effective exclude-newer solver configuration for channels resolved with

    fn exclude_newer_config_with_channel_config(
        &self,

    ) -> Result<Option<rattler_solve::ExcludeNewer>, ParseChannelError> {

    /// Returns the effective exclude-newer solver configuration with absolute cutoffs.
    fn exclude_newer_config_resolved(
        &self,
    ) -> Result<Option<ResolvedExcludeNewer>, ParseChannelError> {
        self.exclude_newer_config_resolved_with_channel_config(&ChannelConfig::default_with_root_dir(
            PathBuf::from("."),
        ))
    }

    /// Returns the effective exclude-newer solver configuration with absolute cutoffs for
    /// channels resolved with the provided channel configuration.
    fn exclude_newer_config_resolved_with_channel_config(
        &self,
        channel_config: &ChannelConfig,
    ) -> Result<Option<ResolvedExcludeNewer>, ParseChannelError> {
        let mut exclude_newer = self
            .exclude_newer_raw()
            .map(|config| ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(config.cutoff()));

        for channel in self.prioritized_channels().into_values() {
            let Some(channel_exclude_newer) = channel.exclude_newer else {
                continue;
            };

            let config = exclude_newer.get_or_insert_with(|| {
                ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(DateTime::<Utc>::MAX_UTC)
            });

            let channel_url = channel.channel.clone().into_base_url(channel_config)?;

            *config = match channel_exclude_newer {
                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => {
                    config.clone().with_channel_cutoff(channel_url.to_string(), dt)
                }
                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => config.clone().with_channel_cutoff(
                    channel_url.to_string(),
                    ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration).cutoff(),
                ),
            };
        }

        for (name, package_exclude_newer) in &self
            .workspace_manifest()
            .workspace
            .exclude_newer_package_overrides
        {
            let config = exclude_newer.get_or_insert_with(|| {
                ResolvedExcludeNewer::from_datetime(DateTime::<Utc>::MAX_UTC)
            });

            *config = match package_exclude_newer {
                ExcludeNewer::Timestamp(dt) => {
                    config.clone().with_package_cutoff(name.clone(), *dt)
                }
                ExcludeNewer::Duration(duration) => config
                    .clone()
                    .with_package_cutoff(name.clone(), ExcludeNewer::Duration(*duration).cutoff()),
            };
        }

        Ok(exclude_newer)
    }
